local FPSValue  = createStat("FPS")
local CPUValue  = createStat("CPU %")
local PingValue = createStat("PING")

local frames = 0
local last = os.clock()

RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
    frames += 1
    local now = os.clock()
    if now - last >= 1 then
        FPSValue.Text = tostring(frames)
        frames = 0
        last = now
    end
end)

task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(0.5) do
        pcall(function()
            local ping = Stats.Network.ServerStatsItem["Data Ping"]:GetValue()
            PingValue.Text = tostring(math.floor(ping))

            -- CPU giáº£ láº­p nháº¹ (á»•n Ä‘á»‹nh)
            local cpu = math.clamp(Stats:GetTotalMemoryUsageMb() / 50, 1, 100)
            CPUValue.Text = tostring(math.floor(cpu))
        end)
    end
end)


local dragging = false
local dragStart, startPos

Frame.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
    if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1
    or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
        dragging = true
        dragStart = input.Position
        startPos = Frame.Position
    end
end)

Frame.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
    if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1
    or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
        dragging = false
    end
end)

UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
    if dragging and (
        input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement
        or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch
    ) then
        local delta = input.Position - dragStart
        Frame.Position = UDim2.new(
            startPos.X.Scale,
            startPos.X.Offset + delta.X,
            startPos.Y.Scale,
            startPos.Y.Offset + delta.Y
        )
    end
end)

local Smooth = {}
Smooth.last = os.clock()
Smooth.avgDelta = 1/60
Smooth.alpha = 0.15

local clampSpike = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(delta)
    if delta > 0.08 then
        return Smooth.avgDelta
    end
    return delta
end)

RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
    local now = os.clock()
    local delta = now - Smooth.last
    Smooth.last = now

    delta = clampSpike(delta)
    Smooth.avgDelta = Smooth.avgDelta + (delta - Smooth.avgDelta) * Smooth.alpha
end)

RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function(delta)
    local smoothDelta = Smooth.avgDelta
    local drift = math.abs(delta - smoothDelta)
    if drift > 0.012 then
        smoothDelta = (smoothDelta + delta) * 0.5
        Smooth.avgDelta = smoothDelta
    end
end)

task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        task.wait(0.017)
    end
end)

if not LocalPlayer.Character then
    LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()
end


local WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE or function(f) return f end
local islclosure = islclosure or function(f) return type(f) == "function" end
local setupvalue = setupvalue or debug.setupvalue

if not debug.getupvalues then
    debug.getupvalues = function(f)
        local t, i = {}, 1
        while true do
            local n, v = debug.getupvalue(f, i)
            if not n then break end
            t[i] = v
            i = i + 1
        end
        return t
    end
end

local function safeGetConnections(event)
    if not getconnections then return {} end
    local ok, r = pcall(getconnections, event)
    return (ok and r) or {}
end

local function disableConn(conn)
    if conn.Disable then 
        pcall(function() conn:Disable() end)
    elseif conn.Disconnect then 
        pcall(function() conn:Disconnect() end) 
    end
end

local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer

local Alive = workspace:FindFirstChild("Alive") or workspace:WaitForChild("Alive")
local Runtime = workspace:FindFirstChild("Runtime") or workspace:WaitForChild("Runtime")

local swordInstancesInstance = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Shared", 9e9):WaitForChild("ReplicatedInstances", 9e9):WaitForChild("Swords", 9e9)

local oldIdentity = (getthreadidentity and getthreadidentity()) or 2
if setthreadidentity then setthreadidentity(2) end

local success, swordInstances = pcall(require, swordInstancesInstance)

if setthreadidentity then setthreadidentity(oldIdentity) end

if not success then return end

local getSlashName = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(swordName)
    local slashName = swordInstances:GetSword(swordName)
    return (slashName and slashName.SlashName) or "SlashEffect"
end)

if not getgenv().equipHooked then
    getgenv().originalEquipSwordTo = swordInstances.EquipSwordTo
    swordInstances.EquipSwordTo = function(self, char, swordName)
        if getgenv().skinChangerEnabled and getgenv().changeSwordModel and char == LocalPlayer.Character then
            swordName = getgenv().swordModel
        end
        return getgenv().originalEquipSwordTo(self, char, swordName)
    end
    getgenv().equipHooked = true
end

local setSword = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    if not getgenv().skinChangerEnabled then return end
    
    pcall(function() setupvalue(getgenv().originalEquipSwordTo, 3, false) end)
    
    if getgenv().changeSwordModel and LocalPlayer.Character then
        swordInstances:EquipSwordTo(LocalPlayer.Character, getgenv().swordModel)
    end
    
    if getgenv().changeSwordAnimation and getgenv().swordsController then
        getgenv().swordsController:SetSword(getgenv().swordAnimations)
    end
end)

getgenv().myParryHandler = function(...)
    if setthreadidentity then setthreadidentity(2) end
    local args = {...}
    
    if tostring(args[4]) == LocalPlayer.Name then
        if getgenv().skinChangerEnabled and getgenv().changeSwordFX then
            args[1] = getgenv().slashName
            args[3] = getgenv().swordFX
        end
    end
    
    if getgenv().playParryFunc then
        return getgenv().playParryFunc(unpack(args))
    end
end

if not getgenv().fxHooked then
    ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.ParrySuccessAll.OnClientEvent:Connect(getgenv().myParryHandler)
    getgenv().fxHooked = true
end

task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(0.2) do
        if not getgenv().skinChangerEnabled then continue end

        local fireConns = safeGetConnections(ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.FireSwordInfo.OnClientEvent)
        for i = #fireConns, 1, -1 do
            local conn = fireConns[i]
            if conn.Function and islclosure(conn.Function) then
                local upvalues = debug.getupvalues(conn.Function)
                if type(upvalues[1]) == "table" and upvalues[1].SetSword then
                    local controller = upvalues[1]
                    getgenv().swordsController = controller
                    
                    if not controller.isHooked then
                        local oldSet = controller.SetSword
                        controller.SetSword = function(self, anim)
                            if getgenv().skinChangerEnabled and getgenv().changeSwordAnimation then
                                anim = getgenv().swordAnimations
                            end
                            return oldSet(self, anim)
                        end
                        controller.isHooked = true
                        
                        if getgenv().changeSwordAnimation then
                            oldSet(controller, getgenv().swordAnimations)
                        end
                    end
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        local parryConns = safeGetConnections(ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.ParrySuccessAll.OnClientEvent)
        for i = #parryConns, 1, -1 do
            local conn = parryConns[i]
            if conn.Function and conn.State == true then
                local info = debug.getinfo(conn.Function)
                if info and info.name == "parrySuccessAll" then
                    getgenv().playParryFunc = conn.Function
                    disableConn(conn)
                end
            end
        end
        
        local clientConns = safeGetConnections(ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.ParrySuccessClient.Event)
        for i = #clientConns, 1, -1 do
            local conn = clientConns[i]
            if conn.State == true then
                local info = debug.getinfo(conn.Function)
                if info and info.name == "parrySuccessAll" then
                    disableConn(conn)
                end
            end
        end
    end
end)

if getgenv().swordFX then
    getgenv().slashName = getSlashName(getgenv().swordFX)
end

getgenv().updateSword = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    if getgenv().changeSwordFX and getgenv().swordFX then
        getgenv().slashName = getSlashName(getgenv().swordFX)
    end
    setSword()
end)

LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(character)
    if not getgenv().skinChangerEnabled then return end
    
    local hrp = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart", 5)
    if not hrp then return end
    
    task.wait(1)
    pcall(setSword)
end)

task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(0.5) do
        if not getgenv().skinChangerEnabled then continue end
        local char = LocalPlayer.Character
        if char and getgenv().swordModel and not char:FindFirstChild(getgenv().swordModel) then
            pcall(setSword)
        end
    end
end)

local System = {
    __properties = {

System.detection = System.detection or {}

local Hash, UUID, ParryRemote

for _, T in pairs(getgc(true)) do
    if type(T) ~= "table" then continue end
    local R, S3 = rawget(T, 0), rawget(T, 3)
    if typeof(R) == "Instance" and R:IsA("RemoteEvent") and type(S3) == "table" then
        local H, U_idx = rawget(S3, 2), rawget(S3, 3)
        if type(H) == "string" and type(U_idx) == "number" then
            Hash, UUID = H, rawget(T, U_idx + 4)
        end
    end
    local F, EU = rawget(T, 2), rawget(T, 3)
    if not ParryRemote and type(F) == "function" and type(EU) == "string" and type(rawget(T, 0)) == "table" then
        if string.len(EU) >= 36 and string.sub(EU, 9, 9) == "-" then
            local Net = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Packages._Index["sleitnick_net@0.1.0"].net
            ParryRemote = Net:FindFirstChild("RE/" .. F(string.gsub(EU, "-", ""), EU))
        end
    end
    if Hash and UUID and ParryRemote then break end
end

if ParryRemote and Hash and UUID then
    local Players = game:GetService("Players")
    local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
    local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
    
    -- [CỐT LÕI MỚI]: Cache data 1 lần duy nhất mỗi frame để chống lag CPU
    local current_frame_data = {}
    local current_frame_cam = workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame
    
    RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        current_frame_cam = workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame
        table.clear(current_frame_data)
        for _, p in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if p ~= LocalPlayer and p.Character and p.Character.PrimaryPart then
                current_frame_data[p.Name] = p.Character.PrimaryPart.Position
            end
        end
    end)

    getgenv().Parry = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
        if not LocalPlayer.Character or not LocalPlayer.Character.PrimaryPart then return end
        
        local screenSize = workspace.CurrentCamera.ViewportSize
        local aim = {
            (screenSize.X * 0.5) + math.random(-50, 50),
            (screenSize.Y * 0.5) + math.random(-50, 50)
        }

        -- Bắn thẳng với data siêu tươi (fresh) từ Heartbeat, tốn 0% CPU
        ParryRemote:FireServer(UUID, Hash, 0.5, current_frame_cam, current_frame_data, aim, false)
    end)

    print("Founded Remote:", ParryRemote.Name, "| Hash:", Hash)
    print("O(1) Parry Optimization Active")
else
    warn("Failed to hook remote")
end

    title.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    title.TextSize = 14
    title.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
    title.TextColor3 = ball_velocity.__config.colors.text_primary
    title.Parent = header

    local content = Instance.new("Frame")
    content.Size = UDim2.new(1, -24, 1, -44)
    content.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 38)
    content.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    content.Parent = main

    local stat = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(y, label, color)
        local l = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        l.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 16)
        l.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, y)
        l.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        l.Text = label
        l.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
        l.TextSize = 11
        l.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        l.TextColor3 = ball_velocity.__config.colors.text_secondary
        l.Parent = content

        local v = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        v.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 22)
        v.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, y + 14)
        v.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        v.Text = "0.0"
        v.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        v.TextSize = 18
        v.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        v.TextColor3 = color
        v.Parent = content
        return v
    end)

    local current_value = stat(0, "Current Speed", ball_velocity.__config.colors.accent_green)
    local peak_value = stat(42, "Peak Speed", ball_velocity.__config.colors.accent_orange)

    --// DRAG LOGIC (FIXED)
    local drag_start, start_pos

    header.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1
        or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            ball_velocity.__state.is_dragging = true
            drag_start = input.Position
            start_pos = main.Position
        end
    end)

    UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
        if ball_velocity.__state.is_dragging
        and input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.Change then
            local delta = input.Position - drag_start
            main.Position = UDim2.new(
                start_pos.X.Scale,
                start_pos.X.Offset + delta.X,
                start_pos.Y.Scale,
                start_pos.Y.Offset + delta.Y
            )
        end
    end)

    UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1
        or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            ball_velocity.__state.is_dragging = false
        end
    end)

    return gui, current_value, peak_value
end)

--// START
ball_velocity.start = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    if ball_velocity.__state.active then return end
    ball_velocity.__state.active = true
    ball_velocity.__state.ball_data = {}

    local gui, current, peak = ball_velocity.create_gui()
    ball_velocity.__state.gui = gui

    System.__properties.__connections.ball_velocity =
        RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
            local ball = System.ball.get()
            if not ball then
                current.Text = "0.0"
                peak.Text = "0.0"
                return
            end

            local z = ball:FindFirstChild("zoomies")
            if not z then
                current.Text = "0.0"
                return
            end

            local speed = z.VectorVelocity.Magnitude
            ball_velocity.__state.ball_data[ball] =
                math.max(ball_velocity.__state.ball_data[ball] or 0, speed)

            current.Text = string.format("%.1f", speed)
            peak.Text = string.format("%.1f", ball_velocity.__state.ball_data[ball])
        end)
end)

--// STOP
ball_velocity.stop = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    ball_velocity.__state.active = false
    if System.__properties.__connections.ball_velocity then
        System.__properties.__connections.ball_velocity:Disconnect()
        System.__properties.__connections.ball_velocity = nil
    end
    if ball_velocity.__state.gui then
        ball_velocity.__state.gui:Destroy()
        ball_velocity.__state.gui = nil
    end
    ball_velocity.__state.ball_data = {}
end)


System.animation = {}

System.animation.play_grab_parry = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    if not System.__properties.__play_animation then
        return
    end
    
    local character = LocalPlayer.Character
    if not character then return end
    
    local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass('Humanoid')
    local animator = humanoid and humanoid:FindFirstChildOfClass('Animator')
    if not humanoid or not animator then return end
    
    local sword_name
    if getgenv().skinChangerEnabled then
        sword_name = getgenv().swordAnimations
    else
        sword_name = character:GetAttribute('CurrentlyEquippedSword')
    end
    if not sword_name then return end
    
    local sword_api = ReplicatedStorage.Shared.SwordAPI.Collection
    local parry_animation = sword_api.Default:FindFirstChild('GrabParry')
    if not parry_animation then return end
    
    local sword_data = ReplicatedStorage.Shared.ReplicatedInstances.Swords.GetSword:Invoke(sword_name)
    if not sword_data or not sword_data['AnimationType'] then return end
    
    for _, object in pairs(sword_api:GetChildren()) do
        if object.Name == sword_data['AnimationType'] then
            if object:FindFirstChild('GrabParry') or object:FindFirstChild('Grab') then
                local animation_type = object:FindFirstChild('GrabParry') and 'GrabParry' or 'Grab'
                parry_animation = object[animation_type]
            end
        end
    end
    
    if System.__properties.__grab_animation and System.__properties.__grab_animation.IsPlaying then
        System.__properties.__grab_animation:Stop()
    end
    
    System.__properties.__grab_animation = animator:LoadAnimation(parry_animation)
    System.__properties.__grab_animation.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Action4
    System.__properties.__grab_animation:Play()
end)

System.ball = {}

System.ball.get = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    local balls = workspace:FindFirstChild('Balls')
    if not balls then return nil end
    
    for _, ball in pairs(balls:GetChildren()) do
        if ball:GetAttribute('realBall') then
            ball.CanCollide = false
            return ball
        end
    end
    return nil
end)

System.ball.get_all = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    local balls_table = {}
    local balls = workspace:FindFirstChild('Balls')
    if not balls then return balls_table end
    
    for _, ball in pairs(balls:GetChildren()) do
        if ball:GetAttribute('realBall') then
            ball.CanCollide = false
            table.insert(balls_table, ball)
        end
    end
    return balls_table
end)

System.player = {}

local Closest_Entity = nil

System.player.get_closest = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    if not Alive then return nil end
    
    local player_character = LocalPlayer.Character
    
    -- Early exit if player character doesn't exist
    if not player_character or not player_character.PrimaryPart then 
        Closest_Entity = nil
        return nil 
    end
    
    local player_pos = player_character.PrimaryPart.Position
    local min_distance_sq = math.huge  -- DĂ¹ng squared distance, nhanh hÆ¡n
    local closest_entity = nil
    
    for _, entity in pairs(Alive:GetChildren()) do
        -- Combined check Ä‘á»ƒ skip sá»›m
        if entity ~= player_character and entity:IsA("Model") and entity.PrimaryPart then
            local entity_pos = entity.PrimaryPart.Position
            
            -- TĂ­nh squared distance (bá» sqrt = nhanh hÆ¡n ~30%)
            local dx = player_pos.X - entity_pos.X
            local dy = player_pos.Y - entity_pos.Y
            local dz = player_pos.Z - entity_pos.Z
            local distance_sq = dx*dx + dy*dy + dz*dz
            
            if distance_sq < min_distance_sq then
                min_distance_sq = distance_sq
                closest_entity = entity
            end
        end
    end
    
    Closest_Entity = closest_entity
    return closest_entity
end)

System.player.get_closest_to_cursor =WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    if not Alive then return nil end

    local player_character = LocalPlayer.Character
    if not player_character or not player_character.PrimaryPart then
        return nil
    end

    local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera
    if not camera then return nil end

    local mouse_location = UserInputService:GetMouseLocation()
    if not mouse_location then return nil end

    local ray = camera:ViewportPointToRay(mouse_location.X, mouse_location.Y)
    local ray_dir = ray.Direction
    local camera_pos = camera.CFrame.Position
    
    local best_score = -math.huge
    local best_player = nil

    for _, player in pairs(Alive:GetChildren()) do
        if player ~= player_character and player:IsA("Model") then
            local hrp = player.PrimaryPart or player:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            if hrp then
                local delta = hrp.Position - camera_pos
                local distance_sq = delta.X*delta.X + delta.Y*delta.Y + delta.Z*delta.Z
                
                if distance_sq < 250000 then
                    local dir = delta.Unit
                    local dot = ray_dir:Dot(dir)
                    
                    if dot > 0.2 then
                        local distance_factor = 1 - math.sqrt(distance_sq) / 500
                        local score = (dot * 0.6) + (distance_factor * 0.4)
                        
                        if score > best_score then
                            best_score = score
                            best_player = player
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
    
    return best_player
end)

System.curve = {}

System.curve.get_cframe = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera
    local root = LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart')
    if not root then return camera.CFrame end

    -- Lấy target gần cursor nhất
    local targetPart
    local closest = System.player.get_closest_to_cursor()
    if closest and closest:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart') then
        targetPart = closest.HumanoidRootPart
    end

    local target_pos = targetPart
        and targetPart.Position
        or (root.Position + camera.CFrame.LookVector * 100)

    local curve_functions = {
        -- Mode 1: Camera (Camera CFrame trực tiếp)
        function()
            return camera.CFrame
        end,

        -- Mode 2: Random (offset ngẫu nhiên, tránh quá thẳng)
        function()
            local direction = (target_pos - root.Position).Unit
            local random_offset
            local attempts = 0
            repeat
                random_offset = Vector3.new(
                    math.random(-4000, 4000),
                    math.random(-4000, 4000),
                    math.random(-4000, 4000)
                )
                local curve_direction = (target_pos + random_offset - root.Position).Unit
                local dot = direction:Dot(curve_direction)
                attempts = attempts + 1
            until dot < 0.95 or attempts > 10
            return CFrame.new(root.Position, target_pos + random_offset)
        end,

        -- Mode 3: Straight (nhắm vào player gần cursor nhất — từ Parry_Type 'Straight')
        function()
            local Mouse_Location = UserInputService:GetMouseLocation()
            local Mouse_Vector = Vector2.new(Mouse_Location.X, Mouse_Location.Y)
            local Aimed_Player = nil
            local Closest_Distance = math.huge

            for _, v in pairs(workspace.Alive:GetChildren()) do
                if v ~= LocalPlayer.Character and v.PrimaryPart then
                    local screenPos, isOnScreen = camera:WorldToScreenPoint(v.PrimaryPart.Position)
                    if isOnScreen then
                        local dist = (Mouse_Vector - Vector2.new(screenPos.X, screenPos.Y)).Magnitude
                        if dist < Closest_Distance then
                            Closest_Distance = dist
                            Aimed_Player = v
                        end
                    end
                end
            end

            if Aimed_Player then
                return CFrame.new(root.Position, Aimed_Player.PrimaryPart.Position)
            else
                return CFrame.new(root.Position, target_pos)
            end
        end,

        -- Mode 4: Backwards (ngược hướng camera, có độ cao — từ Parry_Type 'Backwards')
        function()
            local direction = (root.Position - target_pos).Unit
            local backwards_pos = root.Position + direction * 10000 + Vector3.new(0, 1000, 0)
            return CFrame.new(camera.CFrame.Position, backwards_pos)
        end,

        -- Mode 5: Down / Slowball (thẳng xuống dưới)
        function()
            return CFrame.new(root.Position, target_pos + Vector3.new(0, -9e18, 0))
        end,

        -- Mode 6: High / Up (thẳng lên trên)
        function()
            return CFrame.new(root.Position, target_pos + Vector3.new(0, 9e18, 0))
        end,

        -- Mode 7: Left (trái theo RightVector của camera — từ Parry_Type 'Left')
        function()
            local left_pos = camera.CFrame.Position - camera.CFrame.RightVector * 10000
            return CFrame.new(camera.CFrame.Position, left_pos)
        end,

        -- Mode 8: Right (phải theo RightVector của camera — từ Parry_Type 'Right')
        function()
            local right_pos = camera.CFrame.Position + camera.CFrame.RightVector * 10000
            return CFrame.new(camera.CFrame.Position, right_pos)
        end,

        -- Mode 9: RandomTarget (nhắm vào một player ngẫu nhiên trên màn hình — từ Parry_Type 'RandomTarget')
        function()
            local candidates = {}
            for _, v in pairs(workspace.Alive:GetChildren()) do
                if v ~= LocalPlayer.Character and v.PrimaryPart then
                    local screenPos, isOnScreen = camera:WorldToScreenPoint(v.PrimaryPart.Position)
                    if isOnScreen then
                        table.insert(candidates, v)
                    end
                end
            end
            if #candidates > 0 then
                local pick = candidates[math.random(1, #candidates)]
                return CFrame.new(root.Position, pick.PrimaryPart.Position)
            else
                return camera.CFrame
            end
        end,
    }

    local mode = System.__properties.__curve_mode
    if curve_functions[mode] then
        return curve_functions[mode]()
    else
        return camera.CFrame
    end
end)

System.parry = {}

System.parry.execute = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    if System.__properties.__parries > 10000 or not LocalPlayer.Character then
        return
    end
    
    local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera
    local success, mouse = pcall(function()
        return UserInputService:GetMouseLocation()
    end)
    
    if not success then return end
    
    local vec2_mouse = {mouse.X, mouse.Y}
    local is_mobile = System.__properties.__is_mobile
    
    -- [VĂ Lá»–I 1]: Gá»­i Ä‘Ăºng Vector3 (Position) thay vĂ¬ tá»a Ä‘á»™ mĂ n hĂ¬nh (ScreenPoint)
    local event_data = {}
    if Alive then
        for _, entity in pairs(Alive:GetChildren()) do
            if entity.PrimaryPart then
                -- Láº¥y tháº³ng Position thá»±c táº¿ trong khĂ´ng gian 3D
                event_data[entity.Name] = entity.PrimaryPart.Position
            end
        end
    end
    
    local curve_cframe = System.curve.get_cframe()
    
    if not System.__properties.__first_parry_done then
        for _, connection in pairs(getconnections(LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Hotbar.Block.Activated)) do
            connection:Fire()
        end
        System.__properties.__first_parry_done = true
        return
    end

    local properties = System.__properties

    if properties.__parries > 10000 then return end

    -- [VĂ Lá»–I 2]: ThĂªm cÆ¡ cháº¿ chá»‘ng phĂ¡t hiá»‡n Aim tÄ©nh (Randomize Aim)
    local final_aim_target
    if is_mobile then
        local viewport = camera.ViewportSize
        final_aim_target = {
            (viewport.X * 0.5) + math.random(-30, 30) + math.random(), 
            (viewport.Y * 0.5) + math.random(-30, 30) + math.random()
        }
    else
        final_aim_target = {
            vec2_mouse[1] + math.random(-15, 15) + math.random(),
            vec2_mouse[2] + math.random(-15, 15) + math.random()
        }
    end

    -- [VĂ Lá»–I 3]: Trá»±c tiáº¿p báº¯n lá»‡nh FireServer chuáº©n xĂ¡c nháº¥t lĂªn Server
    if ParryRemote and Hash and UUID then
        ParryRemote:FireServer(
            UUID, 
            Hash, 
            0.5,               -- Báº¯t buá»™c lĂ  0.5
            curve_cframe,      -- GĂ³c nhĂ¬n 
            event_data,        -- Vector3 má»¥c tiĂªu
            final_aim_target,  -- Tá»a Ä‘á»™ chuá»™t Ä‘Ă£ lĂ m giáº£
            false
        )
    end

    -- Update parry counter with decay
    properties.__parries = properties.__parries + 1
    task.delay(0.5, function()
        if properties.__parries > 0 then
            properties.__parries = properties.__parries - 1
        end
    end)
end)

System.parry.keypress = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    if System.__properties.__parries > 10000 or not LocalPlayer.Character then
        return
    end

    -- Gá»i luĂ´n hĂ m execute vá»«a Ä‘Æ°á»£c vĂ¡ lá»—i á»Ÿ trĂªn thay vĂ¬ hĂ m PF() cÅ© Ä‘Ă£ bá»‹ há»ng
    System.parry.execute()

    if System.__properties.__parries > 10000 then return end
    
    System.__properties.__parries = System.__properties.__parries + 1
    task.delay(0.5, function()
        if System.__properties.__parries > 0 then
            System.__properties.__parries = System.__properties.__parries - 1
        end
    end)
end)

-- // aqqqqq

System.parry.execute_action = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    System.animation.play_grab_parry()
    System.parry.execute()
end)

local linear_predict = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(start_value, end_value, t)
    t = math.clamp(t, 0, 1)
    return start_value + (end_value - start_value) * t
end)

System.detection.is_curved = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    if not System.detection.__ball_properties then
        System.detection.__ball_properties = {
            __previous_velocity = {},
            __curving            = tick(),
            __lerp_radians       = 0,
            __last_warping       = tick(),
            __curve_strength     = 0,
            __curve_start_time   = 0
        }
    end

    local ball_properties = System.detection.__ball_properties
    local Ball = System.ball.get()
    if not Ball then return false end

    local Zoomies = Ball:FindFirstChild('zoomies')
    if not Zoomies then return false end

    local Velocity = Zoomies.VectorVelocity
    local Speed = Velocity.Magnitude
    if Speed < 1 then return false end

    local Ball_Direction = Velocity.Unit
    -- [BUG FIX] playerPos là Part, phải dùng .Position
    local playerPos = LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character.PrimaryPart
    if not playerPos then return false end
    local ballPos = Ball.Position
    local Direction = (playerPos.Position - ballPos).Unit
    local Dot = Direction:Dot(Ball_Direction)

    -- Lưu lịch sử velocity để tính góc thay đổi
    table.insert(ball_properties.__previous_velocity, Velocity)
    if #ball_properties.__previous_velocity > 8 then
        table.remove(ball_properties.__previous_velocity, 1)
    end

    local max_angle_change = 0
    local avg_angle_change = 0

    if #ball_properties.__previous_velocity >= 4 then
        local angles = {}
        for i = 1, #ball_properties.__previous_velocity - 1 do
            local prev_dir = ball_properties.__previous_velocity[i].Unit
            local curr_dir = ball_properties.__previous_velocity[i + 1].Unit
            local angle_change = math.acos(math.clamp(prev_dir:Dot(curr_dir), -1, 1))
            local angle_deg = math.deg(angle_change)
            table.insert(angles, angle_deg)
            if angle_deg > max_angle_change then
                max_angle_change = angle_deg
            end
        end

        local sum = 0
        for _, v in ipairs(angles) do sum = sum + v end
        avg_angle_change = sum / #angles

        ball_properties.__curve_strength = math.min(max_angle_change / 40, 1)
    end

    -- Phát hiện Tornado
    if Ball:FindFirstChild('AeroDynamicSlashVFX') then
        Debris:AddItem(Ball.AeroDynamicSlashVFX, 0)
        System.__properties.__tornado_time = tick()
        ball_properties.__curve_strength = 0.95
    end

    local Runtime = workspace.Runtime
    if Runtime:FindFirstChild('Tornado') then
        local tornadoDuration = (Runtime.Tornado:GetAttribute("TornadoTime") or 1) + 0.314
        if (tick() - System.__properties.__tornado_time) < tornadoDuration then
            ball_properties.__curve_strength = 0.9
            return true
        end
    end

    -- ── BỔ SUNG: Ping + Distance + ReachTime layers ─────────────────────────
    local ok, Ping = pcall(function()
        return game:GetService("Stats").Network.ServerStatsItem["Data Ping"]:GetValue()
    end)
    if not ok then Ping = 50 end

    local Distance     = (playerPos.Position - ballPos).Magnitude
    local ReachTime    = Distance / math.max(Speed, 1) - Ping / 1000
    local DotThreshold = 0.5 - Ping / 1000

    local SpeedThreshold        = math.min(Speed / 100, 40)
    local BallDistanceThreshold = 15 - math.min(Distance / 1000, 15) * SpeedThreshold

    if Speed > 160 and ReachTime < Ping / 10 / 133.33 then
        if Speed < 300 then
            BallDistanceThreshold = math.max(BallDistanceThreshold - 15, 15)
        elseif Speed < 600 then
            BallDistanceThreshold = math.max(BallDistanceThreshold - 16, 16)
        elseif Speed < 1000 then
            BallDistanceThreshold = math.max(BallDistanceThreshold - 17, 17)
        elseif Speed < 1500 then
            BallDistanceThreshold = math.max(BallDistanceThreshold - 19, 19)
        else
            BallDistanceThreshold = math.max(BallDistanceThreshold - 20, 20)
        end
    end

    if Distance < BallDistanceThreshold then return false end

    -- Layer: ReachTime warp check
    local adjustedReachTime = ReachTime / 133.33
    if Speed < 300 then
        if tick() - ball_properties.__curving < adjustedReachTime * 1.2   then return true end
    elseif Speed < 450 then
        if tick() - ball_properties.__curving < adjustedReachTime * 1.21  then return true end
    elseif Speed < 600 then
        if tick() - ball_properties.__curving < adjustedReachTime * 1.335 then return true end
    else
        if tick() - ball_properties.__curving < adjustedReachTime * 1.5   then return true end
    end

    -- Layer: DotDifference check
    local DirectionDifference = Ball_Direction - Velocity.Unit
    if DirectionDifference.Magnitude > 0 then
        local DirectionSimilarity = Direction:Dot(DirectionDifference.Unit)
        local DotDifference       = Dot - DirectionSimilarity
        if DotDifference > DotThreshold then return true end
    end

    -- Layer: LerpRadians warp-time
    local ClampedDot = math.clamp(Dot, -1, 1)
    local Radians    = math.deg(math.asin(ClampedDot))
    ball_properties.__lerp_radians = ball_properties.__lerp_radians + (Radians - ball_properties.__lerp_radians) * 0.8

    if Speed < 300 then
        if ball_properties.__lerp_radians > 0.02 then ball_properties.__last_warping = tick() end
        if tick() - ball_properties.__last_warping < ReachTime * 1.19 then return true end
    else
        if ball_properties.__lerp_radians > 0.018 then ball_properties.__last_warping = tick() end
        if tick() - ball_properties.__last_warping < ReachTime * 1.5  then return true end
    end

    -- Layer: So sánh với 2 velocity cũ nhất
    if #ball_properties.__previous_velocity >= 4 then
        local v1 = ball_properties.__previous_velocity[1]
        local v2 = ball_properties.__previous_velocity[2]
        if v1 and v1.Magnitude > 0 then
            local diff1 = Ball_Direction - v1.Unit
            if diff1.Magnitude > 0 then
                if (Dot - Direction:Dot(diff1.Unit)) > DotThreshold then return true end
            end
        end
        if v2 and v2.Magnitude > 0 then
            local diff2 = Ball_Direction - v2.Unit
            if diff2.Magnitude > 0 then
                if (Dot - Direction:Dot(diff2.Unit)) > DotThreshold then return true end
            end
        end
    end

    -- Layer: Backwards curve detection
    local horizDir = Vector3.new(
        playerPos.Position.X - ballPos.X, 0, playerPos.Position.Z - ballPos.Z
    )
    if horizDir.Magnitude > 0 then
        horizDir = horizDir.Unit
        local horizBallDir = Vector3.new(Ball_Direction.X, 0, Ball_Direction.Z)
        if horizBallDir.Magnitude > 0 then
            horizBallDir = horizBallDir.Unit
            local backwardsAngle = math.deg(math.acos(math.clamp((-horizDir):Dot(horizBallDir), -1, 1)))
            if backwardsAngle > 60 then return true end
        end
    end
   
    local is_curving = false

    if max_angle_change > 15 then
        is_curving = true
    elseif max_angle_change > 8 and Dot < 0.6 then
        is_curving = true
    elseif max_angle_change > 5 and Dot < 0.4 then
        is_curving = true
    end

    if not is_curving then
        Ball:SetAttribute("curve_start_time", nil)
        ball_properties.__curve_start_time = 0
    elseif is_curving and not Ball:GetAttribute("curve_start_time") and ball_properties.__curve_start_time == 0 then
        local start_time = tick()
        Ball:SetAttribute("curve_start_time", start_time)
        ball_properties.__curve_start_time = start_time
    end

    return is_curving
end)

System.detection.get_curve_strength = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    if not System.detection.__ball_properties then
        return 0
    end
    return System.detection.__ball_properties.__curve_strength or 0
end)

    end
end)

ReplicatedStorage.Packages._Index["sleitnick_net@0.1.0"].net["RE/SlashesOfFuryEnd"].OnClientEvent:Connect(function()
    System.__properties.__slashesoffury_active = false
    System.__properties.__slashesoffury_count = 0
end)

ReplicatedStorage.Packages._Index["sleitnick_net@0.1.0"].net["RE/SlashesOfFuryParry"].OnClientEvent:Connect(function()
    System.__properties.__slashesoffury_count = System.__properties.__slashesoffury_count + 1
end)

ReplicatedStorage.Packages._Index["sleitnick_net@0.1.0"].net["RE/SlashesOfFuryCatch"].OnClientEvent:Connect(function()
    spawn(function()
        while System.__properties.__slashesoffury_active and System.__properties.__slashesoffury_count < maxParryCount do
            if System.__config.__detections.__slashesoffury then
                System.parry.execute()
                task.wait(parryDelay)
            else
                break
            end
        end
    end)
end)

Runtime.ChildAdded:Connect(function(Object)
    if System.__config.__detections.__phantom then
        if Object.Name == "maxTransmission" or Object.Name == "transmissionpart" then
            local Weld = Object:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("WeldConstraint")
            if Weld then
                local Character = LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                if Character and Weld.Part1 == Character.HumanoidRootPart then
                    local CurrentBall = System.ball.get()
                    Weld:Destroy()
                    
                    if CurrentBall then
                        local FocusConnection
                        FocusConnection = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
                            local Highlighted = CurrentBall:GetAttribute("highlighted")
                            
                            if Highlighted == true then
                                ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.AbilityButtonPress:Fire()
                                System.__properties.__parried = true
                                
                                task.delay(1, function()
                                    System.__properties.__parried = false
                                end)
                                
                            elseif Highlighted == false then
                                FocusConnection:Disconnect()
                            end
                        end)
                        
                        task.delay(3, function()
                            if FocusConnection and FocusConnection.Connected then
                                FocusConnection:Disconnect()
                            end
                        end)
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
end)

ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.ParrySuccessAll.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(_, root)
if not root or not root.Parent then return end
if root.Parent == LocalPlayer.Character then return end
if not Alive or root.Parent.Parent ~= Alive then return end

-- Debounce  
local props = System.__properties  
props.__last_parry = props.__last_parry or 0  
if tick() - props.__last_parry < 0.05 then return end  
props.__last_parry = tick()  

local closest = System.player.get_closest()  
local ball = System.ball.get()  
if not ball or not closest or not closest.PrimaryPart then return end  
if closest == LocalPlayer.Character then return end  

local character = LocalPlayer.Character  
local rootPart = character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")  
if not rootPart then return end  

local player_pos = rootPart.Position  
local ball_pos = ball.Position  

local to_ball = player_pos - ball_pos  
if to_ball.Magnitude == 0 then return end  

local distance = to_ball.Magnitude  
local target_distance =  
    (player_pos - closest.PrimaryPart.Position).Magnitude  

if distance > 15 or target_distance > 15 then return end  

local zoomies = ball:FindFirstChild("zoomies")  
if not zoomies then return end  

local velocity = zoomies.VectorVelocity  
if velocity.Magnitude == 0 then return end  

local dot = to_ball.Unit:Dot(velocity.Unit)  
if dot <= 0.1 then return end  

if System.detection.is_curved() then  
    System.parry.execute_action()  
end  

if props.__grab_animation then  
    props.__grab_animation:Stop()  
end

end)
  
-- Cleanup (always executes)  
if System.__properties.__grab_animation then  
    System.__properties.__grab_animation:Stop()  
end


ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.ParrySuccess.OnClientEvent:Connect(function()
    if not Alive or LocalPlayer.Character.Parent ~= Alive then
        return
    end
    
    if System.__properties.__grab_animation then
        System.__properties.__grab_animation:Stop()
    end
end)

ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.ParrySuccessAll.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(a, b)
    local Primary_Part = LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character.PrimaryPart
    if not Primary_Part then return end

    local Ball = System.ball.get()
    if not Ball then return end

    local Zoomies = Ball:FindFirstChild('zoomies')
    if not Zoomies then return end

    local Velocity = Zoomies.VectorVelocity
    local Speed = Velocity.Magnitude
    if Speed <= 1 then return end

    local Player_Pos = Primary_Part.Position
    local Ball_Pos = Ball.Position
    local Distance = (Player_Pos - Ball_Pos).Magnitude

    local Ball_Direction = Velocity.Unit
    local Direction = (Player_Pos - Ball_Pos).Unit
    local Dot = Direction:Dot(Ball_Direction)

    local Ping_Factor = Stats.Network.ServerStatsItem['Data Ping']:GetValue() * 0.001
    local Speed_Threshold = math.min(Speed * 0.01, 40)
    local Reach_Time = Distance / Speed - Ping_Factor

    -- FIX 1: dùng * thay vì +
    local Ball_Distance_Threshold = 15 - math.min(Distance * 0.001, 15) * Speed_Threshold

    -- FIX 2: < thay vì >
    if Speed > 160 and Reach_Time < Ping_Factor * 100 then
        if Speed < 300 then
            Ball_Distance_Threshold = math.max(Ball_Distance_Threshold - 15, 15)
        elseif Speed < 600 then
            Ball_Distance_Threshold = math.max(Ball_Distance_Threshold - 16, 16)
        elseif Speed < 1000 then
            Ball_Distance_Threshold = math.max(Ball_Distance_Threshold - 17, 17)
        elseif Speed < 1500 then
            Ball_Distance_Threshold = math.max(Ball_Distance_Threshold - 19, 19)
        else
            Ball_Distance_Threshold = math.max(Ball_Distance_Threshold - 20, 20)
        end
    end

    -- FIX 3: guard nil trước khi truy cập
    if b ~= Primary_Part and Distance > Ball_Distance_Threshold then
        if System.detection.__ball_properties then
            System.detection.__ball_properties.__curving = tick()
        end
    end
end)

System.manual_spam = {}

local msthreads = {}
local msconns   = {}

System.manual_spam.loop_stop = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    System.__properties.__manual_spam_enabled = false

    for _, t in ipairs(msthreads) do
        pcall(function() task.cancel(t) end)
    end
    msthreads = {}

    for _, c in ipairs(msconns) do
        pcall(function() c:Disconnect() end)
    end
    msconns = {}
end)

System.manual_spam.loop_start = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    System.manual_spam.loop_stop()

    System.__properties.__manual_spam_enabled = true

    local function fire()
        local parry_fn = getgenv().Parry
        if not parry_fn then return end
        parry_fn() parry_fn() parry_fn() parry_fn()
    end

    -- 3 coroutine liên tục như Eclipse
    local t1 = coroutine.create(function()
        while System.__properties.__manual_spam_enabled do
            fire() task.wait(0)
        end
    end)
    coroutine.resume(t1)
    table.insert(msthreads, t1)

    local t2 = coroutine.create(function()
        while System.__properties.__manual_spam_enabled do
            fire() task.wait(0)
        end
    end)
    coroutine.resume(t2)
    table.insert(msthreads, t2)

    local t3 = coroutine.create(function()
        while System.__properties.__manual_spam_enabled do
            fire() task.wait(0)
        end
    end)
    coroutine.resume(t3)
    table.insert(msthreads, t3)

    -- RenderStepped
    table.insert(msconns, RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
        if System.__properties.__manual_spam_enabled then
            fire() fire() fire()
        end
    end))

    -- Stepped
    table.insert(msconns, RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
        if System.__properties.__manual_spam_enabled then
            fire() fire() fire()
        end
    end))

    -- PreSimulation (= PreSimulation của Eclipse là R.PreSimulation)
    table.insert(msconns, RunService.PreSimulation:Connect(function()
        if System.__properties.__manual_spam_enabled then
            fire() fire() fire()
        end
    end))

    -- Animation fix
    if getgenv().ManualSpamAnimationFix then
        table.insert(msconns, RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
            if not System.__properties.__manual_spam_enabled then return end
            local anim_fn = System.animation and System.animation.play_grab_parry
            if anim_fn then anim_fn() end
        end))
    end
end)

System.manual_spam.start = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    System.manual_spam.loop_start()
end)

System.manual_spam.stop = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    System.manual_spam.loop_stop()
end)

System.auto_spam = {}

local RunService   = cloneref and cloneref(game:GetService("RunService")) or game:GetService("RunService")
local Stats        = cloneref and cloneref(game:GetService("Stats")) or game:GetService("Stats")
local VECTOR3_ZERO = Vector3.zero

local as_conns   = {}

System.auto_spam.start = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    for _, c in ipairs(as_conns) do pcall(function() c:Disconnect() end) end
    table.clear(as_conns)

    if setfpscap then setfpscap(240) end

    System.__properties.__auto_spam_enabled = true
    System.__properties.__is_spamming       = false

    local anim_fn      = System.animation and System.animation.play_grab_parry
    local ping_stat    = Stats.Network.ServerStatsItem["Data Ping"]
    local LocalPlayer  = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
    local my_name      = tostring(LocalPlayer)
    
    local last_zoomies = nil
    local last_ball    = nil
    
    -- Biến cache để không phải tính toán 2 lần
    local is_clashing  = false 
    local last_ping_update = 0
    local cached_ping  = 50

    -- 1. HÀM TÍNH TOÁN (Chỉ gọi 1 lần mỗi frame để tiết kiệm 50% CPU)
    local function update_clash_state()
        if not System.__properties.__auto_spam_enabled then 
            is_clashing = false
            return 
        end
        
        local character = LocalPlayer.Character
        local primary_part = character and character.PrimaryPart
        if not primary_part or character:GetAttribute("Pulsed") then 
            is_clashing = false
            return 
        end

        System.player.get_closest()
        local closest = Closest_Entity
        if not closest or not closest.PrimaryPart then 
            is_clashing = false
            return 
        end

        local ball = System.ball.get()
        if not ball then 
            is_clashing = false
            return 
        end

        if ball ~= last_ball then
            last_ball = ball
            last_zoomies = ball:FindFirstChild("zoomies")
        end

        local speed       = ((last_zoomies and last_zoomies.VectorVelocity) or ball.AssemblyLinearVelocity or VECTOR3_ZERO).Magnitude
        local ball_target = ball:GetAttribute("target")
        
        if ball_target ~= my_name and ball_target ~= closest.Name then 
            is_clashing = false
            return 
        end

        local my_pos      = primary_part.Position
        local ball_dist   = (my_pos - ball.Position).Magnitude
        local entity_dist = (my_pos - closest.PrimaryPart.Position).Magnitude

        -- Tối ưu: Chỉ lấy Ping mỗi 0.25s (để không làm khựng game)
        local now = os.clock()
        if now - last_ping_update > 0.25 then
            local ok, p_val = pcall(function() return ping_stat:GetValue() end)
            if ok then cached_ping = p_val / 10 end
            last_ping_update = now
        end

        local spam_range = math.max(cached_ping / 10, 15) + (speed / 5)
        local hit_count  = System.__properties.__parries or 0
        
        is_clashing = ((hit_count > 1) or (ball_dist < 15.0)) and (entity_dist <= spam_range)
        System.__properties.__is_spamming = is_clashing
    end

    -- 2. HÀM XẢ: Gọi thẳng, KHÔNG DÙNG task.spawn rác
    local function do_fire()
        local parry_fn = getgenv().Parry
        if parry_fn then
            -- Gọi tuần tự siêu mượt. Hàm Parry O(1) chạy mất 0.0001ms
            -- Gọi ntn nhanh và sạch hơn task.spawn 1000 lần.
            parry_fn(); parry_fn(); parry_fn(); parry_fn();
            parry_fn(); parry_fn(); parry_fn(); parry_fn();
        end

        if getgenv().AutoSpamAnimationFix and anim_fn then
            task.defer(anim_fn)
        end
    end

    -- 3. HEARTBEAT: Tính toán 1 lần + Xả đạn
    table.insert(as_conns, RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        update_clash_state()
        if is_clashing then do_fire() end
    end))

    -- 4. PRERENDER: KHÔNG tính toán lại, CHỈ xả đạn theo cache
    table.insert(as_conns, RunService.PreRender:Connect(function()
        if is_clashing then do_fire() end
    end))
end)

System.auto_spam.stop = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    System.__properties.__auto_spam_enabled = false
    System.__properties.__is_spamming       = false
    for _, c in ipairs(as_conns) do pcall(function() c:Disconnect() end) end
    table.clear(as_conns)
end)

System.autoparry = {}

local CONSTANTS = {
    MAX_TRACK_DIST_SQ  = 300 * 300,
    CLASH_DISTANCE     = 30,
    CLASH_DIST_SQ      = 30 * 30,
    PING_UPDATE_RATE   = 0.15,
    ANIMATION_COOLDOWN = 0.10,
}

local best_threat = {
    ball = nil, distance = 0, speed = 0, dot = 0, tti = 0,
    target = nil, is_training = false, velocity = Vector3.zero
}

local ResetBestThreat = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    best_threat.ball        = nil
    best_threat.distance    = 0
    best_threat.speed       = 0
    best_threat.dot         = 0
    best_threat.tti         = 0
    best_threat.target      = nil
    best_threat.is_training = false
    best_threat.velocity    = Vector3.zero
end)

local ping_samples = {}
local prev_ping    = 50
local last_update  = 0

local get_avg_ping = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    local ok, raw = pcall(function()
        return game:GetService("Stats").Network.ServerStatsItem["Data Ping"]:GetValue()
    end)
    local ping = ok and raw or 50
    table.insert(ping_samples, ping)
    if #ping_samples > 10 then table.remove(ping_samples, 1) end
    local sum = 0
    for _, v in ipairs(ping_samples) do sum = sum + v end
    return sum / #ping_samples
end)

local update_divisor = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    local now = tick()
    if now - last_update < 0.5 then return end
    last_update = now

    local properties = System.__properties
    local accuracy   = math.clamp(properties.__accuracy or 1, 1, 100)
    local avg_ping   = get_avg_ping()
    local jitter     = math.abs(avg_ping - prev_ping)
    prev_ping        = avg_ping

    local divisor
    if accuracy <= 10 then divisor = 0.90 + (accuracy - 1)  * 0.020
    elseif accuracy <= 20 then divisor = 1.08 + (accuracy - 10) * 0.018
    elseif accuracy <= 30 then divisor = 1.26 + (accuracy - 20) * 0.022
    elseif accuracy <= 40 then divisor = 1.48 + (accuracy - 30) * 0.024
    elseif accuracy <= 50 then divisor = 1.72 + (accuracy - 40) * 0.026
    elseif accuracy <= 60 then divisor = 1.98 + (accuracy - 50) * 0.024
    elseif accuracy <= 70 then divisor = 2.22 + (accuracy - 60) * 0.020
    elseif accuracy <= 80 then divisor = 2.42 + (accuracy - 70) * 0.016
    elseif accuracy <= 90 then divisor = 2.58 + (accuracy - 80) * 0.014
    elseif accuracy <= 95 then divisor = 2.72 + (accuracy - 90) * 0.024
    else divisor = 2.84 + (accuracy - 95) * 0.032 end

    local ping_offset  = math.min(avg_ping / 300, 1.667) * 0.6
    local ping_scale   = 0.2 + (accuracy / 100) * 0.8
    local jitter_bonus = math.clamp(jitter / 200, 0, 0.25)
    local speed_bonus  = math.clamp(((properties.__ball_speed or 100) - 100) / 2000, 0, 0.4)

    if properties.__spam_mode then
        divisor = (divisor + ping_offset * ping_scale + jitter_bonus + speed_bonus) * 0.7
    else
        divisor = divisor + ping_offset * ping_scale + jitter_bonus + speed_bonus
    end

    properties.__divisor_multiplier = divisor
end)

local EvaluateParryDecision = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(threat, is_curving, in_clash_zone, char_pos, ping_seconds, properties)
    if properties.__interaction_locked[threat.ball] then return false end

    local trigger_parry  = false
    local effective_ping = ping_seconds + 0.055
    local time_to_impact = threat.distance / math.max(threat.speed, 1)

    if is_curving then
        local curve_buffer = in_clash_zone and 0.035 or 0.08
        if time_to_impact <= (effective_ping + curve_buffer) then
            trigger_parry = true
        end
    else
        if threat.speed >= 800 then
            local clash_spam_tti = effective_ping + 0.15 + (threat.speed / 2500)
            if threat.dot > 0.4 and time_to_impact <= clash_spam_tti then
                trigger_parry = true
            end
        else
            local speed_comp = (threat.speed / 100) * 0.025
            if threat.dot > 0.6 and time_to_impact <= (effective_ping + speed_comp) then
                trigger_parry = true
            end

            if not trigger_parry then
                local predicted_pos   = threat.ball.Position + (threat.velocity * effective_ping)
                local future_distance = (char_pos - predicted_pos).Magnitude

                local speed_diff    = math.max(threat.speed - 9.5, 0)
                local base_div      = threat.is_training and 2.2  or 1.55
                local mult_div      = threat.is_training and 0.0018 or 0.0011
                local speed_divisor = (base_div + speed_diff * mult_div) * (properties.__divisor_multiplier or 1)

                local hitbox_radius = math.max(threat.speed / speed_divisor, 14.0)

                if future_distance <= hitbox_radius or threat.distance <= hitbox_radius then
                    trigger_parry = true
                end
            end
        end
    end

    if trigger_parry then
        properties.__interaction_locked[threat.ball] = true
    end

    return trigger_parry
end)

-- Biến chứa Remote đã bypass
local OptimizedRemote = { Remote = nil, Hash = nil, UUID = nil }

local function FindParryRemote()
    if OptimizedRemote.Remote then return end
    for _, T in pairs(getgc(true)) do
        if type(T) ~= "table" then continue end
        local R, S3 = rawget(T, 0), rawget(T, 3)
        if typeof(R) == "Instance" and R:IsA("RemoteEvent") and type(S3) == "table" then
            local H, Uidx = rawget(S3, 2), rawget(S3, 3)
            if type(H) == "string" and type(Uidx) == "number" then
                OptimizedRemote.Hash = H
                OptimizedRemote.UUID = rawget(T, Uidx + 4)
            end
        end

        local F, EU = rawget(T, 2), rawget(T, 3)
        if not OptimizedRemote.Remote and type(F) == "function" and type(EU) == "string" and type(rawget(T, 0)) == "table" then
            if string.len(EU) == 36 and string.sub(EU, 9, 9) == "-" then
                local Net = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Packages._Index["sleitnick_net@0.1.0"].net
                OptimizedRemote.Remote = Net:FindFirstChild("RE/" .. F(string.gsub(EU, "-", ""), EU))
            end
        end
        if OptimizedRemote.Hash and OptimizedRemote.UUID and OptimizedRemote.Remote then break end
    end
end

System.autoparry.start = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    if System.__properties.__connections.__autoparry then
        System.__properties.__connections.__autoparry:Disconnect()
        System.__properties.__connections.__autoparry = nil
    end

    FindParryRemote() -- Đảm bảo tìm Remote ngay khi bật

    System.__properties.__autoparry_enabled  = true
    System.__properties.__last_parry_time    = 0
    System.__properties.__ball_targets       = System.__properties.__ball_targets or {}
    System.__properties.__interaction_locked = System.__properties.__interaction_locked or {}
    System.__properties.__ping_history       = {}

    local RunService  = game:GetService("RunService")
    local Stats       = game:GetService("Stats")
    local Players     = game:GetService("Players")
    local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
    local ENV         = getgenv()

    local last_ping_update      = 0
    local smoothedPing          = 50
    local active_training_balls = {}
    local training_folder       = workspace:FindFirstChild("TrainingBalls")
    local tornado_time          = 0

    if training_folder then
        for _, child in ipairs(training_folder:GetChildren()) do
            if child and child:GetAttribute("realBall") then active_training_balls[child] = true end
        end
        System.__properties.__connections.__training_added = training_folder.ChildAdded:Connect(function(child)
            if child and child:GetAttribute("realBall") then active_training_balls[child] = true end
        end)
        System.__properties.__connections.__training_removed = training_folder.ChildRemoved:Connect(function(child)
            active_training_balls[child] = nil
            System.__properties.__ball_targets[child]       = nil
            System.__properties.__interaction_locked[child] = nil
        end)
    end

    local current_frame_data = {}
    local current_frame_cam = workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame
    System.__properties.__connections.__autoparry_cache = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        current_frame_cam = workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame
        table.clear(current_frame_data)
        for _, p in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if p ~= LocalPlayer and p.Character and p.Character.PrimaryPart then
                current_frame_data[tostring(p.Name)] = p.Character.PrimaryPart.Position
            end
        end
    end)

    local connection
    connection = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
        if not System.__properties.__autoparry_enabled then return end

        local character = LocalPlayer.Character
        local root_part = character and character.PrimaryPart
        if not character or not root_part then return end

        local now_clock  = os.clock()
        local char_pos   = root_part.Position
        local local_name = LocalPlayer.Name

        local Singularity_Cape = root_part:FindFirstChild('SingularityCape')
        if Singularity_Cape then return end

        if ENV.InfinityDetection      and System.__properties.__infinity_active      then return end
        if ENV.DeathSlashDetection    and System.__properties.__deathslash_active    then return end
        if ENV.TimeHoleDetection      and System.__properties.__timehole_active      then return end
        if ENV.SlashesOfFuryDetection and System.__properties.__slashesoffury_active then return end

        update_divisor()

        if now_clock - last_ping_update >= CONSTANTS.PING_UPDATE_RATE then
            local currentPing = Stats.Network.ServerStatsItem['Data Ping']:GetValue() / 10
            table.insert(System.__properties.__ping_history, currentPing)
            if #System.__properties.__ping_history > 5 then table.remove(System.__properties.__ping_history, 1) end
            local s = 0
            for _, v in ipairs(System.__properties.__ping_history) do s = s + v end
            smoothedPing = #System.__properties.__ping_history > 0 and (s / #System.__properties.__ping_history) or 10
            last_ping_update = now_clock
        end

        local all_balls = System.ball.get_all()
        local has_training = next(active_training_balls) ~= nil
        if #all_balls == 0 and not has_training then return end

        ResetBestThreat()

        local ProcessBall = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(Ball, is_training)
            if not Ball.Parent then
                System.__properties.__ball_targets[Ball]       = nil
                System.__properties.__interaction_locked[Ball] = nil
                return
            end

            if Ball:FindFirstChild("ComboCounter") then return end
            if Ball:FindFirstChild('AeroDynamicSlashVFX') then
                game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(Ball.AeroDynamicSlashVFX, 0)
                tornado_time = tick()
            end
            local tornado_runtime = workspace:FindFirstChild("Runtime") and workspace.Runtime:FindFirstChild('Tornado')
            if tornado_runtime then
                local tornado_duration = (tornado_runtime:GetAttribute("TornadoTime") or 1) + 0.314159
                if (tick() - tornado_time) < tornado_duration then return end
            end

            local current_target = Ball:GetAttribute("target")
            if System.__properties.__ball_targets[Ball] ~= current_target then
                System.__properties.__ball_targets[Ball] = current_target
                if current_target == local_name then System.__properties.__interaction_locked[Ball] = false end
            end
            if System.__properties.__interaction_locked[Ball] == nil then
                System.__properties.__interaction_locked[Ball] = (current_target ~= local_name)
            end

            local Zoomies  = Ball:FindFirstChild("zoomies")
            if not Zoomies then return end
            local Velocity = Zoomies.VectorVelocity
            local Speed    = Velocity.Magnitude
            if Speed <= 0 then return end

            local diff_vector = char_pos - Ball.Position
            local dist_sq     = diff_vector:Dot(diff_vector)
            if dist_sq <= 0 or dist_sq > CONSTANTS.MAX_TRACK_DIST_SQ then return end

            local Distance    = math.sqrt(dist_sq)
            local inv_mag     = 1 / Speed
            local vel_unit    = Velocity * inv_mag
            local direction   = diff_vector / Distance
            local dot_product = direction:Dot(vel_unit)

            if dot_product < -0.1 or (current_target ~= local_name and dot_product < 0.1) then return end

            local tti = Distance * inv_mag

            if not best_threat.ball
                or (tti < best_threat.tti and current_target == best_threat.target)
                or (current_target == local_name and best_threat.target ~= local_name)
            then
                best_threat.ball        = Ball
                best_threat.distance    = Distance
                best_threat.speed       = Speed
                best_threat.dot         = dot_product
                best_threat.tti         = tti
                best_threat.target      = current_target
                best_threat.is_training = is_training
                best_threat.velocity    = Velocity
            end
        end)

        for _, Ball in ipairs(all_balls) do ProcessBall(Ball, false) end
        for t_ball in pairs(active_training_balls) do ProcessBall(t_ball, true) end

        if not best_threat.ball then return end

        local ping_seconds = smoothedPing / 1000
        local is_target    = (best_threat.target == local_name)

        local closest_player = System.player.get_closest()
        local cp_part        = closest_player and closest_player.PrimaryPart
        local in_clash_zone  = false
        if cp_part then
            local diff = char_pos - cp_part.Position
            in_clash_zone = (diff:Dot(diff) <= CONSTANTS.CLASH_DIST_SQ)
        end

        local is_curving = false
        if is_target and best_threat.speed > 15 and best_threat.dot < 0.95 then
            is_curving = true
        end

        local trigger_parry = EvaluateParryDecision(best_threat, is_curving, in_clash_zone, char_pos, ping_seconds, System.__properties)

        if trigger_parry then
            local time_since_last = now_clock - (System.__properties.__last_parry_time or 0)
            if time_since_last > CONSTANTS.ANIMATION_COOLDOWN then
                if System.animation and System.animation.play_grab_parry then
                    System.animation.play_grab_parry()
                end
            end

            -- CHÍNH THỨC SỬ DỤNG FIRESERVER TRỰC TIẾP
            if OptimizedRemote.Remote and OptimizedRemote.Hash and OptimizedRemote.UUID then
                local curvecframe = System.curve and System.curve.get_cframe() or current_frame_cam
                local viewport = workspace.CurrentCamera.ViewportSize
                local finalaimtarget = {
                    [1] = (viewport.X / 2) + math.random(-50, 50),
                    [2] = (viewport.Y / 2) + math.random(-50, 50)
                }
                
                OptimizedRemote.Remote:FireServer(
                    OptimizedRemote.UUID, 
                    OptimizedRemote.Hash, 
                    0.5, 
                    curvecframe, 
                    current_frame_data, 
                    finalaimtarget, 
                    false
                )
            else
                -- Fallback lỡ nó ko hook được thì chạy lại cái Find
                FindParryRemote()
            end

            System.__properties.__last_parry_time = now_clock
        end
    end)

    System.__properties.__connections.__autoparry = connection
end)

System.autoparry.stop = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    System.__properties.__autoparry_enabled = false

    if System.__properties.__connections.__autoparry then
        System.__properties.__connections.__autoparry:Disconnect()
        System.__properties.__connections.__autoparry = nil
    end
    if System.__properties.__connections.__autoparry_cache then
        System.__properties.__connections.__autoparry_cache:Disconnect()
        System.__properties.__connections.__autoparry_cache = nil
    end
    if System.__properties.__connections.__training_added then
        System.__properties.__connections.__training_added:Disconnect()
        System.__properties.__connections.__training_added = nil
    end
    if System.__properties.__connections.__training_removed then
        System.__properties.__connections.__training_removed:Disconnect()
        System.__properties.__connections.__training_removed = nil
    end

    System.__properties.__ball_targets       = {}
    System.__properties.__interaction_locked = {}
    System.__properties.__ping_history       = {}
    System.__properties.__last_parry_time    = 0
    ResetBestThreat()
end)

local create_mobile_button = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(name, position_y, color)
    local gui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
    gui.Name = "Sigma" .. name .. "Mobile"
    gui.ResetOnSpawn = false
    gui.IgnoreGuiInset = true
    gui.ZIndexBehavior = Enum.ZIndexBehavior.Sibling
    gui.Parent = gethui()

    local container = Instance.new("Frame")
    container.Size = UDim2.new(0, 200, 0, 100)
    container.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -100, position_y, 0)
    container.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0)
    container.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(35, 40, 90)
    container.BorderSizePixel = 0
    container.Active = true        
    container.Draggable = true    
    container.Parent = gui

    local corner = Instance.new("UICorner")
    corner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 22)
    corner.Parent = container

    local stroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
    stroke.Color = color or Color3.fromRGB(180, 170, 255)
    stroke.Thickness = 2
    stroke.ApplyStrokeMode = Enum.ApplyStrokeMode.Border
    stroke.Parent = container

    local button = Instance.new("TextButton")
    button.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
    button.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    button.Text = ""
    button.AutoButtonColor = false
    button.Active = false          
    button.ZIndex = 2
    button.Parent = container

    local text = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    text.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
    text.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    text.Text = name
    text.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
    text.TextSize = 22
    text.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 240, 255)
    text.ZIndex = 3
    text.Parent = button

    return { gui = gui, bg = container, button = button, text = text }
end)

local destroy_mobile_gui = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(gui_data)
    if gui_data and gui_data.gui then 
        gui_data.gui:Destroy() 
    end
end)

local ManualSpamLabel = SpamSection:AddLabel('Manual Spam')
ManualSpamLabel:AddToggle({
    Default = false,
    Flag = "ManualSpam",
    Callback = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(state)
        if System.__properties.__is_mobile then
            if state then
                if not System.__properties.__mobile_guis.manual_spam then
                    local manual_spam_mobile = create_mobile_button('Spam', 0.8, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255))
                    System.__properties.__mobile_guis.manual_spam = manual_spam_mobile
                    local manual_touch_start = 0
                    local manual_was_dragged = false

                    manual_spam_mobile.button.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
                        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                            manual_touch_start = tick()
                            manual_was_dragged = false
                        end
                    end)

                    manual_spam_mobile.button.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
                        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                            if (tick() - manual_touch_start) > 0.1 then 
                                manual_was_dragged = true 
                            end
                        end
                    end)

                    manual_spam_mobile.button.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
                        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch and not manual_was_dragged then
                            System.__properties.__manual_spam_enabled = not System.__properties.__manual_spam_enabled
                            if System.__properties.__manual_spam_enabled then
                                System.manual_spam.start()
                                manual_spam_mobile.text.Text = "ON"
                                manual_spam_mobile.text.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 100)
                            else
                                System.manual_spam.stop()
                                manual_spam_mobile.text.Text = "Spam"
                                manual_spam_mobile.text.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                end
            else
                System.__properties.__manual_spam_enabled = false
                System.manual_spam.stop()
                destroy_mobile_gui(System.__properties.__mobile_guis.manual_spam)
                System.__properties.__mobile_guis.manual_spam = nil
            end
        else
            System.__properties.__manual_spam_enabled = state
            if state then 
                System.manual_spam.start() 
            else 
                System.manual_spam.stop() 
            end
        end
    end)
})

local FOVLabel = FOVSection:AddLabel("FOV")
FOVLabel:ToolTip("Changes Camera POV")
FOVLabel:AddToggle({
    Default = false,
    Flag = "FOV",
    Callback = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(value)
        getgenv().CameraEnabled = value
        local Camera = workspace.CurrentCamera

        if value then
            getgenv().CameraFOV = getgenv().CameraFOV or 70
            Camera.FieldOfView = getgenv().CameraFOV

            if not getgenv().FOVLoop then
                getgenv().FOVLoop = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
                    if getgenv().CameraEnabled then
                        workspace.CurrentCamera.FieldOfView = getgenv().CameraFOV
                    end
                end)
            end
        else
            Camera.FieldOfView = 70

            if getgenv().FOVLoop then
                getgenv().FOVLoop:Disconnect()
                getgenv().FOVLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end)
})

FOVLabel:AddSlider({
    Min = 50,
    Max = 120,
    Type = "",
    Default = 70,
    Rounding = 0,
    Flag = "Camera_FOV",
    Callback = WYNF_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(value)
        getgenv().CameraFOV = value
        if getgenv().CameraEnabled then
            workspace.CurrentCamera.FieldOfView = value
        end
    end)
})
